/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[getNavigatedUser]    Script Date: 28-03-2024 01:13:42 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
-- exec [dbo].[getNavigatedUser] 
CREATE procedure [dbo].[getNavigatedUser] 
as 
begin
	WITH RankedInteractions AS (
    SELECT 
       *,
        ROW_NUMBER() OVER (PARTITION BY UserId
                           ORDER BY 
                               CASE
							       WHEN PageUrl = 'UW Questions' THEN 1
                                   WHEN PageUrl = 'Mortgagees' THEN 2
                                   WHEN PageUrl = 'Blankets' THEN 3
                                   WHEN PageUrl = 'Buildings/Classifications' THEN 4
								   WHEN PageUrl = 'State Specific Info/Additional Coverages' THEN 5
                                   WHEN PageUrl = 'State Specific Info/Coverages' THEN 6
                                   WHEN PageUrl = 'Locations' THEN 7
								   WHEN PageUrl = 'Locations' THEN 8
                                   WHEN PageUrl = 'Businessowners/Additional Coverages' THEN 9
                                   WHEN PageUrl = 'Businessowners/Coverages' THEN 10
                                   WHEN PageUrl = 'Businessowners/Details' THEN 11
								   WHEN PageUrl = 'Policy Details' THEN 12
                                   ELSE 13
                               END) AS PriorityRank
    FROM  
        [Interactions].[dbo].[CurrentInteractions]
)
SELECT 
  *,
CASE 
	    WHEN  PageUrl = 'UW Questions' THEN 12
        WHEN PageUrl = 'Mortgagees' THEN 11
        WHEN PageUrl = 'Blankets' THEN 10
        WHEN  PageUrl = 'Buildings/Classifications' THEN 9
	    WHEN  PageUrl = 'State Specific Info/Additional Coverages' THEN 8
        WHEN PageUrl = 'State Specific Info/Coverages' THEN 7
		WHEN PageUrl = 'Locations/Location Additional Coverages' THEN 6
        WHEN PageUrl = 'Locations' THEN 5
        WHEN  PageUrl = 'Businessowners/Additional Coverages' THEN 4
        WHEN PageUrl = 'Businessowners/Coverages' THEN 3
        WHEN PageUrl = 'Businessowners/Details' THEN 2
        ELSE 1
    END AS order_C
FROM  
    RankedInteractions
WHERE 
    PriorityRank = 1
	
ORDER BY 
    order_C desc;

	END
	
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[GetUserPageVisits]    Script Date: 28-03-2024 01:13:42 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[GetUserPageVisits]
As
WITH PageVisits AS (
    SELECT 
        UserId,
        PageUrl,
        SaveDateTime,
        LAG(PageUrl) OVER (PARTITION BY UserId ORDER BY SaveDateTime DESC) AS PreviousPageUrl,
        LEAD(SaveDateTime) OVER (PARTITION BY UserId ORDER BY SaveDateTime DESC) AS NextDateTime
    FROM 
        CurrentInteractions
    --WHERE
    --    UserId = 'anilapkar'
)
SELECT
    UserId,
    PreviousPageUrl AS PageUrl,
    SaveDateTime,
    NextDateTime,
    DATEDIFF(MINUTE, NextDateTime, SaveDateTime) AS TimeSpentMinutes,
	DATEDIFF(SECOND, NextDateTime, SaveDateTime) AS TimeSpentSeconds
FROM
    PageVisits
WHERE
    NextDateTime IS NOT NULL
    AND PageUrl = 'Error';
GO
USE [master]
GO
ALTER DATABASE [Interactions] SET  READ_WRITE 
GO
